{"code":1,"isDone":false,"toInsertArticleList":[{"createdTime":"2020-08-26 01:41:41","updatedTime":"2020-08-26 01:41:41","title":"I Think These Fall Skirt-and-Shoe Pairings Work Every Single Time","link":"http://feeds.whowhatwear.com/~r/WhoWhatWear/~3/zWJTWecol3w/fall-outfits-with-skirts","description":"<p class=\"p1\">For me, getting dressed often revolves around foolproof outfit formulas. Yep—I love to experiment, but <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/fall-capsule-wardrobe\" target=\"_blank\">I'm also a major outfit repeater</a>. Once I find something that works, I know that it's an easy way to get dressed without putting too much thought into what I'm wearing. This summer, <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/shop-like-an-editor-best-trendy-fashion-basics\" target=\"_blank\">some of my favorite combos</a> have been linen pants and tube tops, padded shoulder tees with wide-leg denim shorts, <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/ext?tl=9p810VXRe_5d1xH7JKWpYKqfPxvchqjEOwQOvNqBc9-fVamBiCKmWGCx8Ul9dHf-Ndo1RKqg-cI\" target=\"_blank\">linen dresses with strappy sandals</a>, and bodysuits with slip skirts—outfits I've worn again and again without thinking twice. Looking to fall, though, what are the easy looks I'll be trying out?</p><p class=\"p1\">As a big skirt person, I've been thinking about how I'll transition some of my favorite pieces to the next season. Looking to some of my favorite <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/italian-capsule-wardrobe\" target=\"_blank\">street style looks</a>, I already have plenty of fall outfits with skirts earmarked to put my own spin on in the coming months. Ahead, see the skirt-and-shoe pairings I'll be trying out for myself soon because I love a great outfit shortcut. Trust me—these will never go out of style.</p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/268977/fall-outfits-with-skirts-268977-1598244916805-main.1000x1500uc.jpg\"><figcaption>If you opt for a leather skirt, try a longer version like this one from Nanushka. one of your go-to warm-weather outfits given that it’s very much still summer. But fall is fast approaching, so we figured there could be interest in noting the <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/fall-trends-under-100\" target=\"_blank\">trends</a> that will enter the spotlight soon for a bit of pre-autumn shopping inspiration. While we recently covered everything from the <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/fall-boots\" target=\"_blank\">shoe picks</a> to the <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/dress-trends-for-fall\" target=\"_blank\">dress silhouettes</a> that are bound to leave a mark on the season, we thought we’d also get some insight from a top expert for her insider thoughts on the fall items that will hold strong.</p><p>Naturally, we hit up the head buyer at one of the largest fashion retailers out there. We’re talking about <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/ext?tl=QBnBukeOUUqgfl_Y-KQtUctpbJh8t3ZDydlHVGgA_X9IdFWx-b__5uF2_siCQCAC8vvJfn84KlxCnqswQ9k\" target=\"_blank\">Stephanie Nelson Roberson</a>, the general merchandise manager at <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/ext?tl=M-Kdt8VU53qLRzCXNuPzkKpYp_OzEN0HZeMu9ii7QNQiXVUeMg1hzRyapeIMScRfImvU3Bi_0VWJofh4M4YfIGFCi_IEvcn-OJCpO9VbUKfhwjjTpgKGNl8rxSIVyVLbU652bhwrlng2ab4-V9khpoWn7n6r\" target=\"_blank\">Shopbop</a>. Her day-to-day job is overseeing the buying operation for the brand, so it’s safe to say that she understands merchandise and what will be most popular.</p><p>Intrigued? Keep scrolling for Roberson’s debrief on the six key pieces she thinks could be worth it for the season, complete with a bit of visual inspo on various fashion people. There are endless possibilities to suit everyone's comfort.\"</figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288689/fashion-to-buy-for-fall-288689-1597861843423-main.946x1429uc.jpg\"><figcaption>\"Leather shorts have been a wardrobe staple for me this year. 01:41:41","updatedTime":"2020-08-26 01:41:41","title":"From Gigi Hadid to Lizzo, Stars Love This NYC-Based Bold, Young Brand","link":"http://feeds.whowhatwear.com/~r/WhoWhatWear/~3/VkdzKPT7r6Y/tia-adeola-review","description":"<p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/287150/lcd-shop-review-287150-1588979528759-main.1200x1200uc.gif\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><em><span>Welcome</span><span> to our newest editorial initiative, </span></em><span><a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/tags/who-what-wear-spotlight\" target=\"_blank\">Who What Wear Spotlight</a></span><em><span>, where we'll be using our editorial platform, social following, and ad inventory to turn the spotlight on small businesses that need our support now more than ever. Each week, we'll be highlighting a new fashion or beauty company. If you own a small brand and would like to be considered for the program, <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/ext?tl=0VA6QXK_dsIPEtFbo6Z22JeUCfev4_MA6mjtTCOeBi5LmycHmlu7HDw6f81f377zlLPhdtj4QemNO3xMt17UvWOscJtrMG_BpdZ7nmwNe3UbDrpscXiC19OS-Wr4PwnaM7SNhCKfUnUXtRuEZW4KtldPRg\" target=\"_blank\">please apply here</a>.</span></em></p><p>Some people work their entire lives and see marginal success; some people are just in college when celebrities like Lizzo, Dua Lipa, and Gigi Hadid wear their designs. Teni Adeola is of the latter, and she has no shortage of impressive accomplishments. Among the ones she achieved before graduating from college is debuting her first collection at New York Fashion Week, then under the name Slashed by Tia. She's only 23 years old, but she already felt it was time for her brand to graduate to a more mature name, <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/ext?tl=1qvZE9nQroGGk3H4ZnhTKgX7b3AATBFpprm7CZ0AA0PzMWmsyZhqA9pk\" target=\"_blank\">Tia Adeola</a>.</p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288723/golde-review-1-288723-1597942183391-main.1200x1718uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p>Adeola is no stranger to pushing barriers: It's in the soul of her clothing line. As a Nigerian-born woman, she knows the type of sheer and revealing clothes she creates are taboo and frowned upon, but she sees it as her duty to dismantle those traditional constructs that strip women of their freedom, especially their freedom to express their sexuality. </p><p>And she isn't just restructuring the representation of female bodies in the 21st century, she's taking a foundational era of art history and reimagining it with Black bodies. Take one look at Adeola's designs, and it's immediately obvious how inspired she is by the Italian Renaissance. It lives in her larger-than-life ruffled sets, collars, and balloon sleeves. And it greets you directly on with tees and dresses printed with classic high-art motifs, like the Pietà and royal portraiture, featuring Black individuals in place of the white people who filled those paintings for centuries.</p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288723/golde-review-1-288723-1597942206942-main.1200x1802uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p>Thus, Adeola's designs are statements. So it's no surprise that some of the most groundbreaking stars wear them on stages, in photoshoots, and while out and about for the paparazzi and world to see. SZA, Kali Uchis, and Lorde are among the other celebrities who have worn Adeola's designs—a clear indicator that Adeola has a very exciting future ahead of her. I, for one, can't wait to see where it goes. In the meantime, check out the designs Adeola's most excited about right now and a few more we're super into as well.</p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288723/golde-review-1-288723-1597942228350-main.1200x1737uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><strong>Tell us about yourself and your business.</strong></p><p>I am a 23-year-old womenswear designer. I was raised in Nigeria and am currently based in New York. I started my brand Tia Adeola, which was formerly known as Slashed by Tia, in 2016 while I was studying at The New School and ran the business concurrently with my studies. I graduated last summer and showed my first full collection officially at New York Fashion Week last season. Ever since I have been focusing on building my brand and continuing to study art and design.</p><p><strong>And if you had to sum up your business in five words or less?</strong></p><p>Reclaiming renaissance fashion with a modern twist</p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288723/golde-review-1-288723-1597942250903-main.1200x1798uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><strong>What inspired you to start your business?</strong></p><p>My love for clothing, art, and history.</p><p><strong>How have social-distancing and stay-at-home orders affected your business? How have your priorities shifted?</strong></p><p>It has been bittersweet. It started off confusing and pretty scary, to be honest. They've affected my business in a very positive way. The state of the world at present has led me to dig deeper and ensure there's a message behind my clothing and what it stands for.</p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288723/golde-review-1-288723-1597942272423-main.1200x1801uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><strong>What are two to three of your favorite brands you like to support and why?</strong></p><p><a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/ext?tl=ekV0b1yxdvD4kjmzutQeFtZk4K7sirSDG-UKc-wN5IZ8f-ytT1O3mg\" target=\"_blank\">Amari Carter</a>, who's an amazing Black female designer and a friend of mine, and <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/ext?tl=NB4hCOSKd-rNNLUzteNU0wH98MFxZhVg9FyDr1Z3pg8wqx4\" target=\"_blank\">No Sesso</a> who are signed to the same agency as me.</p><p><strong>What has been your proudest moment as a business owner?</strong></p><p>Being able to show my parents that I'm actually making a profit and not just messing around.</p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288723/golde-review-1-288723-1597942290124-main.1200x1798uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288723/tia-adeola-review-288723-1598291371887-main.850x967uc.jpg\"><figcaption>\"I feel like I played my part by encouraging young people who may not be keen on wearing masks to have one that keeps them and others safe—while looking cool and making a fashion statement.\"</figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288723/tia-adeola-review-288723-1598291405628-main.850x967uc.jpg\"><figcaption>\"This style became a signature statement piece for the brand and a lot of incredible, powerful female artists and creatives have worn it, which played a part in the development of my brand.\"</figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288723/tia-adeola-review-288723-1598293546209-main.850x967uc.png\"><figcaption>\"I shared the Pieta Tank back in February following the F/W 20 show. The image is a painting I learned about while studying art history in high school. While I admired the work of Renaissance artists, such as Botticelli, Caravaggio, and Michelangelo, their art never included people who looked like me. And when they did, it would only be for a portrayal of slaves and jesters. With everything that has been happening in the world, I felt it was important to incorporate Black faces into important art narratives like Mary holding Jesus, so I worked with a graphic designer to reclaim this narrative and make the subjects Black.\"</figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288723/tia-adeola-review-288723-1598292349071-main.850x967uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img 01:41:41","updatedTime":"2020-08-26 01:41:41","title":"This $10 Mascara Is One of the Best I've Tried, and Celebs Love It Too","link":"http://feeds.whowhatwear.com/~r/WhoWhatWear/~3/ryZxBUOvCQ4/loreal-paradise-mascara","description":"<p>As a beauty editor, I am often asked about the areas in which we should save (and splurge) when it comes to our <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/best-anti-aging-night-creams\" target=\"_blank\">beauty routines</a>. Personally, I think spending a little more on a great moisturizer or <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/best-french-serum\" target=\"_blank\">serum with efficacious active ingredients</a>, if your finances allow for it, of course, is a wise beauty choice. However, when it comes to makeup, the areas in which you can save a few pennies and still get high-end results are much greater. The most obvious? Mascara. </p><p>If you ask me, some of the greatest mascara formulas out there are from affordable brands. When it comes to mascara, not only do you not need to spend big to get results, but so many of the expensive formulas leave you questioning what you’re paying for. In fact, I have tried many $37-plus mascaras that do little for my lashes at all and leave me with panda eyes at the end of the day. My absolute go-to that guarantees long-lasting, lengthened, voluminous lashes every single time? L’Oréal Paris <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/ext?tl=dCjMZvFPfdD7fDmF-aZYqPBEj3dXV-tAK8tTamxjLdt29_9sraNc\" target=\"_blank\">Paradise Volumizing Mascara</a> ($10).</p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/286969/loreal-paradise-mascara-286969-1588070970937-image.800x0uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p>When I first heard about the wonders of this mascara a few years ago, it wasn’t available in the UK. Over in the U.S., however, it had firmly established itself as a cult best seller. With celebrity makeup artists like <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/ext?tl=IP-h-4416KxqHavb2oyBwXUKeHRfkwqPFCx6Jg-a3EJ0rploSOiTYxQj-NGTef5zo1M\" target=\"_blank\">Sir John</a> (he’s Beyoncé’s go-to) and <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/ext?tl=08CYLvpqb-QNx_pAbUFWUiVNS0FmcPfQIyUgUIOB5sdn0tvzHjqHZewcyXTWKNIa8IUl8jKsaj5nbuptJqheyg\" target=\"_blank\">Kristofer Buckle</a> (the man behind Blake Lively’s flawless makeup) being big fans of the formula, Paradise Mascara has been cited as one of Hollywood’s favourite makeup products for years.</p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/286969/loreal-paradise-mascara-286969-1588071089219-image.800x0uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p>So when it launched in the UK nearly three years ago, it’s needless to say that people flocked to the aisles of Boots to stock up—including me. And unlike what happens with so many UK makeup launches, the fuss around Paradise never did really die down. Three years on, and it is still a permanent feature in my makeup routine. With just one coat, lashes appear dramatically fuller and longer but maintain a weightless feel that is both comfortable and mess-free. Not only that, but after many hours of wear—even with my oil-prone lids—it failed to smudge.  Even my friends have noted that this isn’t necessarily the case for them, so they opt for the waterproof formula instead, which seems to do the trick.</p><p>If I could only keep hold of one mascara in my rather shamefully large collection, I wouldn’t even hesitate in deciding on this one. Compared to other far more expensive options, I can categorically say that L’Oréal Paris Paradise Volumising Mascara is just about one of the most volumizing and lengthening that money can buy. Don’t believe me? Just ask Beyoncé.</p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/287015/loreal-paradise-mascara-287015-1588204570331-main.800x0uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/287015/loreal-paradise-mascara-287015-1588204507783-main.800x0uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/287015/loreal-paradise-mascara-287015-1588205694325-main.800x0uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/287015/loreal-paradise-mascara-287015-1588205244490-product.1500x1500uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/287015/loreal-paradise-mascara-287015-1588204798479-product.800x800uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/287015/loreal-paradise-mascara-287015-1588204892632-product.0x800uc.png\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/287015/loreal-paradise-mascara-287015-1588205049634-product.0x800uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/287015/loreal-paradise-mascara-287015-1588205727517-main.800x0uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/287015/loreal-paradise-mascara-287015-1588205244029-product.1500x1500uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/287015/loreal-paradise-mascara-287015-1588205245898-product.800x0uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/287015/loreal-paradise-mascara-287015-1588205247189-product.1500x1500uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><em>This post originally appeared on Who What Wear UK. src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/253103/bikini-bottom-styles-253103-1580621984803-main.1200x900uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p>When it comes to swimwear, we’ve shared everything from <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/celebrity-bikini-trends-2020\" target=\"_blank\">the trends celebrities are all over this year</a> to <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/best-australian-swimwear-brands\" target=\"_blank\">the brands I recommend to all my friends </a>and <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/best-bikini-poses\" target=\"_blank\">where to buy the most photogenic suits</a>. While testing out some of the season’s newest styles and silhouettes, I noticed a solid number of swimwear lines are pushing string bikini bottoms. Now, we know what you’re picturing: side-tie bottoms that were popular in early 2000s and typically made with a low-rise fit. But that’s not what I’m referring to. The new wave of string bikinis is way chicer (IMO) and designed without double side ties. Aussie-based swimwear labels like <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/ext?tl=-2gHgs-cfDVhS9b0y-v8ngPgS6vuav07vB8G4ooP00MsP1QAVF6t6S4mV2N9Hj37P_C6duEALQ9PGg\" target=\"_blank\">Asara</a> and <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/ext?tl=ap5Stuh2Cv-BePiHp7EkbcCF6mP81w9aF9GA-OndFYw0N1B7S3dMJwzE\" target=\"_blank\">Bāmba</a> are leading the pack on the updated silhouette.</p><p>Celebrities like Bella Hadid and Victoria’s Secret model Josephine Skriver are already supporting this fresh version of super-thin swimsuit bottoms as well. To really embrace this year's version of the string bikini, we suggest taking note from Skriver and wearing the bottoms hiked up super high. This will not only elongate your legs but also lend a very “Bond-girls look,” <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/best-swimsuit-style-for-longer-legs\" target=\"_blank\">as Skriver told us</a> in an interview. Whether you’re simply curious about the style or ready to add the latest bikini trend to your swimsuit collection, we shopped out the coolest string bikini bottoms online right now. Fall","link":"http://feeds.whowhatwear.com/~r/WhoWhatWear/~3/EYeXfeghNio/retro-fall-fashion-trends","description":"<p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/281921/retro-fall-fashion-trends-281921-1566235488952-main.1080x1080uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p>While grandma dressing is certainly nothing new, there are particular grandma trends that come and go every year. Each season brings a new set of trends that can most likely be found buried in your grandma's closet because fashion is cyclical and what's old is new again faster than you can blink. <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/retro-fashion-trends\" target=\"_blank\">We already brought you the ones that were blowing up for summer</a>, so today we're here to touch on the retro trends that fashion girls will be clamoring for come September. From the colored jewelry you swore you'd never wear to the sweater trend all of your grandparents probably still love, the below five retro trends are going to be everywhere this fall. </p><p><a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/pistachio-colored-jewelry\" target=\"_blank\">Pistachio jewelry</a> and accessories are going to take the fashion world by storm. This season, we're setting aside our gold pieces and basic black bags in favor of pretty colored styles reminiscent of the costume jewelry I used to play with in my grandmother's closet. </p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/281921/retro-fall-fashion-trends-281921-1597379687017-main.1080x1349uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/281921/retro-fall-fashion-trends-281921-1597380919757-main.1080x1349uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/281921/retro-fall-fashion-trends-281921-1597379746563-main.1080x1348uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/281921/retro-fall-fashion-trends-281921-1566181841342-main.1200x1500uc.jpg\"><figcaption>Of course, Instagram's favorite brand has the coolest pistachio bag. </figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/281921/retro-fall-fashion-trends-281921-1597381544409-main.2000x3001uc.jpg\"><figcaption>Costume jewelry, but upgraded.</figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/281921/retro-fall-fashion-trends-281921-1597381671720-main.1128x2000uc.jpg\"><figcaption>The ultimate color pop. </figcaption></figure></p><p>While sweater sets were once reserved for grandparents and prep schools, this fall, fashion girls around the globe will be pairing theirs with everything from vintage denim to loose trousers. You can dip a toe in this trend pool by simply tying a sweater of a similar color family around your shoulders, or dive right in with a matching sweater set.</p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/281921/retro-fall-fashion-trends-281921-1597381727393-main.1080x1350uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/281921/retro-fall-fashion-trends-281921-1597381864684-main.1080x1350uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/281921/retro-fall-fashion-trends-281921-1597382163353-main.1080x1350uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/281921/retro-fall-fashion-trends-281921-1597382752313-main.824x1320uc.jpg\"><figcaption>Does it get any chicer?</figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/281921/retro-fall-fashion-trends-281921-1566182753507-main.800x0uc.jpg\"><figcaption>I'm picturing this with an all-gray outfit—a groutfit, if you will. </figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/281921/retro-fall-fashion-trends-281921-1597382619528-main.1598x2560uc.jpg\"><figcaption>So preppy, yet so chic.</figcaption></figure></p><p>Croc-effect accessories are reminiscent of the belts and handbags I used to see my grandparents wearing—but today they're the luxe-looking trend popping up on everything for fall. The best part about mock croc is that it pretty much <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/affordable-fashion-that-looks-expensive\" target=\"_blank\">always looks expensive</a>, regardless of price tag, and instantly elevates an outfit with its rich texture. </p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/281921/retro-fall-fashion-trends-281921-1597382801047-main.1080x1308uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/281921/retro-fall-fashion-trends-281921-1597382913002-main.1080x1350uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/281921/retro-fall-fashion-trends-281921-1597382965718-main.1080x1350uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/281921/retro-fall-fashion-trends-281921-1597383157200-main.1128x2000uc.jpg\"><figcaption>How different is this shape?</figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/281921/retro-fall-fashion-trends-281921-1597383328572-main.1001x1400uc.jpg\"><figcaption>This color is so pretty.</figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/281921/retro-fall-fashion-trends-281921-1597383450072-main.1128x2000uc.jpg\"><figcaption>These look infinitely more expensive than they are.</figcaption></figure></p><p>Faux-fur jackets are usually associated with tights, chain purses, and walking a small dog (just me?), but as of late, fashion girls are itching to add this textural layer to the top of every fall outfit. It adds interest to your look, and you can typically find nice faux furs at affordable prices. </p><p><figure><img Yes, despite the fact that it’s only the beginning of August and the official start of the autumn is still weeks away. Because even though we’re all for those pretty summer staples (like breezy dresses and the like), it’s always kind of fun to think ahead toward everything the next season has to offer.</p><p>On that note, we thought we’d share some of the <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/dress-trends-for-fall\" target=\"_blank\">key fall 2020 items</a> we’re particularly excited to test out in a few months. To take it one step further, we also thought we’d highlight fall basics on the other end of the spectrum that we may not wear as much due to their somewhat \"outdated\" nature. Of course, this is all based on each editor's personal preference, and you should always wear whatever you love—no matter what anyone says.</p><p>With all that in mind, keep scrolling to check out the fall basics worth noting. every bar beyond annoying and complained about it regularly. Now, having just turned 30, I'm still getting carded every time I order a drink, but I'm doing a whole lot less complaining about it. I definitely have genetics to thank for my youthful appearance, and I also credit my esthetician, <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/ext?tl=E1D8quYrVUwpOxqaPGmVnBHuuHnHSySAxvPT9T1EnT1sExFu-b7eCjU8\" target=\"_blank\">Vanessa Hernandez</a>, who keeps my skin looking fresh with her amazing facials and treatments like <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/ipl-treatment-review\" target=\"_blank\">IPL</a> and <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/benefits-of-micro-needling\" target=\"_blank\">micro-needling.</a></p><p>But I believe another major reason I look younger than I am is my dedication to my skincare routine. A few years ago, I got serious about making my skin a priority in my beauty routine (because really, if your skin looks good, your makeup routine can be quite simple), and I've stuck to it ever since. I also have <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/best-skincare-products-for-redness\" target=\"_blank\">mild rosacea</a>, so that was another key factor in buckling down in the skincare realm. Now that I've mastered it, I love to share the knowledge I've gained from industry experts and estheticians, so if someone asks me about my routine, I give them the long-winded version. I'm not one of those people who say, \"I just drink a lot of water.\" I'll list every detail for those unassuming people who inquire.</p><p>Since I've gotten the question quite a few times now, I figured it would be worth sharing on here in detail in case any of my favorite products have been on your radar and you were curious to find out more. src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288787/michelle-obama-basics-288787-1598339269181-main.1200x901uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p>I don't know about you, but I've been thoroughly enjoying seeing Michelle Obama's real style come to light <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/michelle-obama-post-white-house-style\" target=\"_blank\">post–White House</a>. Now able to dress outside of the confines of a <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/kamala-harris-style\" target=\"_blank\">politics</a>, Obama has been showing off more creative outfits in recent years. Of course, there was her barnstorming fashion tour—er, I mean, <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/michelle-obama-book-tour-outfits\" target=\"_blank\">book tour</a>—of 2019, which made many a headline. But in 2020, we've been able to witness Obama's more laidback style. </p><p>Hard at work on her podcast in recent months, Obama has embraced the casualness that an audio-only medium affords. Translation: She's been wearing lots of comfortable pieces, including flowy cardigans, loose-fitting shirts, and more. That said, she is still doing Zoom interviews for television, so she's been pulling out subtly statement-making items for those appearances. ","link":"http://feeds.whowhatwear.com/~r/WhoWhatWear/~3/tWVDwdUecvU/posse-australian-brand","description":"<p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/288789/posse-australian-brand-288789-1598332185063-main.1200x900uc.jpg\"><figcaption></figcaption></figure></p><p>They say you never get a second chance to make a good first impression, but that's not something Australian brand <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/splash/zk3aBDTnO?w=3697622\" target=\"_blank\">Posse</a> needs to worry about. As soon as the up-and-coming label landed an exclusive at <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/splash/zuyUSqpcY?w=3697624\" target=\"_blank\">Moda Operandi</a>, it started selling like hotcakes. \"We saw an incredible response to Posse when we launched it exclusively in the first week of July,\" the retailer's fashion director, <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/ext?tl=ERsa9wbNNpB-K9MOBymDO1M20TSqzO1Vf20NTayuql8wG7nUjABq4z8PXY8ChvKQ3ZVr8kg\" target=\"_blank\">Lisa Aiken</a>, told Who What Wear. \"In that month alone, the <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/splash/zPhvuh9pq?w=3697609\" target=\"_blank\">Ducky Shorts</a> became an instant sellout success and our top-selling shorts. In fact, the Ducky Shorts sold more than the next five top-selling shorts combined. The even better news is that we re-ordered the style immediately and it’s now on pre-order again—it truly is the short you’ll wear everywhere and the short of summer!\"</p><p>As any brand knows, it's a major coup to earn the stamp of approval from industry veteran Aiken, who has a knack for finding hidden gems. \"I discovered Posse two years ago when they were a direct-to-consumer brand,\" Aiken told us. \"I was really inspired by the Australian label’s commitment to the <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/affordable-sustainable-fashion-brands\" target=\"_blank\">slow fashion movement</a>. The shopper is no longer looking for one and done pieces that they can wear once on a getaway. Instead, she wants easy, transitional pieces that have an extensive lifespan in her closet.\" Posse already counts <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/angelina-jolie-off-white-face-mask\" target=\"_blank\">Angelina Jolie</a>, Romee Strijd, and Dakota Fanning among its celebrity fans. Intrigued? Her latest gym outfit features a familiar brand: Niyama Sol, which J.Lo has collaborated with in the past. I first caught on to the brand because of one of J.Lo's particularly <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/ext?tl=_IBs3bMLSfH0TjO4riVvC_Qdasakr7NzbZepNrLNsH5KXvjBmcg_NZrHLq9Zic_O7b3atDi0igLGyxV0F-5sNMQerxX_WgnxPkcGuA\" target=\"_blank\">glowing reviews</a> in the form of the hashtag #whentheleggingsmakethebootylookgood, referencing Niyama Sol. Something tells us that J.Lo would look good in anything, but her endorsement is definitely convincing. </p><p>Lopez's new selfie, which has racked up 3.7 million likes and counting, also hits on another activewear trend: printed leggings. From H&M and Free People to Tory Burch and Nike, nearly every brand has an iteration of the trend to try. Scroll down to see Jennifer Lopez's leggings, and shop the trend at a variety of price points. my job entailed unboxing, testing, reviewing, and re-testing beauty products. This is not a luxury I take lightly, and while it might seem like a mundane task, my fellow beauty editor, Courtney, and I take a lot of pride in our ability to test and provide thoughtful feedback. (We quite literally receive hundreds of packages each month, so you can understand how this makes up a big part of our job!) Some of this feedback is just between the two of us on Slack, some of it goes to a brand's PR team or even its CEO, and a lot of the time, it comes directly to you! With so many swipes and swatches under my belt, it takes a lot to impress me, and I've admitted on more than one occasion that I've become a bit jaded to the beauty industry's deluge of smoke-and-mirror product launches. Therefore, when a product truly knocks my socks off, it feels like a really big deal, and I can't wait to share every detail. </figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/286787/best-expensive-beauty-products-286787-1587157622747-main.800x0uc.jpg\"><figcaption>Before quarantine, my normal day-to-day was studded with meetings, events, writing, catching up on emails, and everything else being a beauty editor entails. (In addition to, you know, having a life outside of work!) Because of that, it became nearly impossible to try every single product I received, and I had amassed quite a large collection of expensive, sparkly items at home (and in my car, TBH) just waiting to be broken into for testing. I'm lucky enough to be able to work from home right now, and since all of those products are in close proximity and awaiting their potential moment of glory, I've gone full ham, working my way through as many samples as possible. (Some are travel-size samples I've been gifted with in boxes, at events, etc., and some are full-size samples I haven't had a chance to work through yet.) For the past 30 days or so, it's been a fast-and-furious round of beauty-product speed dating, and now, I'm here to report which of these very expensive beauty products I would pay full price for. (In fact, I've already had orders out to Violet Grey and Dermstore to replenish some of my favorites!) Curious to see which expensive beauty products are truly worth the investment? I'm sharing all of my recent favorites below—keep scrolling. </figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/286787/best-expensive-beauty-products-286787-1587157641925-main.1200x1200uc.jpg\"><figcaption>I go back and forth with toners. Sometimes I'm on the train, and sometimes I'm off. But using this best-selling (and very clean!) formula from Indie Lee has me back on board and planning to stay awhile. Right after cleansing, I saturate one of my favorite toning cloths from Renée Rouleau with the solution and then smother my face with. It has high-quality ingredients like aloe, hyaluronic acid, coenzyme q10, and chamomile, and I've noticed a significant uptick in my complexion's dew point and brightness since I started using it every morning and night. </figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/286787/best-expensive-beauty-products-286787-1587157647204-main.1200x1200uc.jpg\"><figcaption>Trust me—the fact that this masque runs for a spine-tingling $100 is not lost on me, and I wouldn't recommend it if I didn't feel it was worth every last penny. Since it comes as a powder, you combine just a tiny bit with water until it transforms into a luxe, mask-friendly paste. It has delicious, organic, wild-harvested ingredients (think nutmeg, vanilla, cacao, cayenne, viamin C, cinnamon, clays, and charcoal) that work harmoniously to immediately perk up the circulation in my complexion, and it's even helped clear some stubborn blemishes I've been at war with for months. Fun fact: You can also use it as a spot treatment!</figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/286787/best-expensive-beauty-products-286787-1587157650291-main.1200x1200uc.jpg\"><figcaption>Every single time I see a celebrity or model run through their nighttime skin routine, this popular (but very expensive) cleanser seems to make an appearance. This cleansing formula starts off as a fine-grain powder cleanser that transforms into pillowy foam once you add water. Enzymes play the MVP by loosening and lifting away dead, dry skin and removing every last trace of makeup or excess sebum or skin residue. </figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/286787/best-expensive-beauty-products-286787-1587157657161-main.1200x1200uc.jpg\"><figcaption>I fell in love with this serum after receiving a sample post-facial from celebrity esthetician Shani Darden. Now, I use it every morning and night, and my skin has been smoother, less red, and significantly more hydrated and glowy. I blame the all-star mix of plumping hyaluronic acid, skin-strengthening vitamin B5, healing Centella Asiatica, and hyperpigmentation-lessening mushroom extract. Plus, it helps calm any irritation or puffiness, lift and tighten fine lines, and reduce dark shadows.</figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/286787/best-expensive-beauty-products-286787-1587157666917-main.1200x1200uc.jpg\"><figcaption>I know I just talked about an eye cream, but my beauty-loving soul wouldn't feel right without talking about this anti-aging option too. I've noticed a decrease in the lift and brightness of my eyes since I ran out, and I can't wait to restock. This one is especially great if you're prone to dryness and flaking, as it has a lovely rich formula that brims with hyaluronic acid, vitamins A, C, and E (which all help with circles and discoloration!) plus the brand's signature blend of peptides and TNS for extra anti-aging perks. </figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/286787/best-expensive-beauty-products-286787-1587157672354-main.1200x1200uc.jpg\"><figcaption>I've loved this mask for quite some time, but I ran out of my big gilded tub quite some time ago. We know the feeling. But that doesn’t mean we can’t celebrate the change in seasons and embrace the <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/fall-fashion-trends-2020\" target=\"_blank\">latest wave of fall trends</a>. While restocking your wardrobe may not feel feasible or even necessary this year, we’re excited to try out the earthy, muted, and moody tones of autumn with an <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/how-to-do-an-at-home-manicure\" target=\"_blank\">at-home manicure</a>. That’s right—even if you can’t remember the last time you had a professional tend to your tips and toes, this year’s lineup of fall trends is easy enough to DIY. </span></p><p><span>To get a jump start on the season, we reached out to a few of our favorite nail experts to hear firsthand what to expect in terms of colors, innovations, and trends this fall. Think of it as an at-home mani consultation that will help guide you through the season ahead. Even better? You’ll know exactly what to ask for when nail salons reopen in your area—just remember to <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/nice-smelling-hand-sanitisers\" target=\"_blank\">sanitize</a>, wear a <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/face-masks\" target=\"_blank\">face mask</a>, and tip generously. </span></p><p>Until then, keep scrolling for inspiration and advice from our pros in New York and Los Angeles.</p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/281221/fall-nail-trends-281221-1598043382327-main.933x810uc.jpg\"><figcaption>“I’ve always gravitated towards blues for fall,” shared Lisa Logan, consulting manicurist for Nails Inc. and owner of The Nail Suite in Harlem, New York. Brittney Boyce, a consulting nail artist for Orly based in L.A., agrees, noting she thinks denim-inspired blues will be big this season. </figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img like Spiritual Gangster.\"</figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/281221/fall-nail-trends-281221-1598043492421-main.800x0uc.jpg\"><figcaption>Nocturnal blues think people will also be gravitating toward edgier nudes, something other than a classic beige or pink,” predicts Jin Soon Choi, the expert nail artist and founder of JinSoon nail polish based in New All our pros concurred, each sharing a different go-to shade. </figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/281221/fall-nail-trends-281221-1598043509922-main.800x0uc.jpg\"><figcaption>\"Milieu is an unexpected taupe shade that is just as neutral but looks much more modern,\" advises Choi.</figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/281221/fall-nail-trends-281221-1598043515157-main.800x0uc.jpg\"><figcaption>\"This quad helps you achieve the perfect look whether you want an ombré nude moment or prefer to stick to one shade,\" recommends Logan. </figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/281221/fall-nail-trends-281221-1598037554396-main.800x0uc.jpg\"><figcaption>Boyce recommends this gorgeous mauve-nude to her clients of all skin tones. </figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/281221/fall-nail-trends-281221-1598037625427-main.800x0uc.jpg\"><figcaption>This new shade from Olive & June's recently launched fall collection is also broadly appealing. </figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/281221/fall-nail-trends-281221-1598034330912-main.1080x1080uc.jpg\"><figcaption>Earth tones are huge for fall among the fashion set. “This fall, we are going to be seeing a lot of earthy-inspired shades,” predicts Mazz Hanna, the L.A.-based celebrity manicurist and founder of Mazz Hanna Beauty.  Boyce concurs, explaining, “With the pandemic going on for so long, we want colors that are more grounding.” We couldn’t agree more.</figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/281221/fall-nail-trends-281221-1598043532960-main.800x0uc.jpg\"><figcaption>\"For a more muted nail look that still makes a statement, I love Essie's Take Me to Thread,\" says Hanna.</figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/281221/fall-nail-trends-281221-1598038035727-main.800x800uc.jpg\"><figcaption>We're fans of this desert-inspired, warm terra-cotta hue. </figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/281221/fall-nail-trends-281221-1598043543216-main.800x0uc.jpg\"><figcaption>Mushroom-inspired shades also work as a neutral for fall.</figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/281221/fall-nail-trends-281221-1598038307505-main.800x0uc.jpg\"><figcaption>Aligned with the fashion industry’s trend toward earth tones, everyone is predicting nature-inspired greens will be in favor for fall manicures.</figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/281221/fall-nail-trends-281221-1598034397044-main.1080x1350uc.jpg\"><figcaption>On the other side of the color wheel, our pros anticipate a wide range of reds dominating the DIY-manicure scene this season. Inspired by fashion weeks past, Choi shares, “I expect to see a selection of beautiful reds, from the classic blue tone to hot orange-reds. This was popular amongst designers such as Marc Jacobs and Calvin Klein at their NYFW shows.”</figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/281221/fall-nail-trends-281221-1598040159772-main.800x0uc.jpg\"><figcaption>You really can't go wrong with a classic red.</figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/281221/fall-nail-trends-281221-1598043564365-main.800x0uc.jpg\"><figcaption>Choi favors deep, wine-colored reds for fall.</figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/281221/fall-nail-trends-281221-1598040025903-main.800x0uc.jpg\"><figcaption>\"I'm obsessed with Orly's Wild Abandon,\" confesses Hanna. \"It's a new take on that old classic, and the long-lasting formula plus patented brush makes professional application achievable at home,\" she explains.</figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/281221/fall-nail-trends-281221-1598034497682-main.1080x1080uc.jpg\"><figcaption>Similarly, Choi is excited to see black nails back in the mix come autumn. “Black is always a great shade for fall and winter. It can go with many different styles. A shiny black manicure is very modern and chic, while a cool, chipped finish (such as the manicure we did this past season for Khaite) gives an edge to your look.”</figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/281221/fall-nail-trends-281221-1598043587168-main.800x0uc.jpg\"><figcaption>The name of this polish speaks for itself.</figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/281221/fall-nail-trends-281221-1598040284729-main.800x0uc.jpg\"><figcaption>Feeling the grunge trend? Yes, please. </figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/281221/fall-nail-trends-281221-1598034535578-main.1080x1349uc.jpg\"><figcaption>For those who have used this time at home to perfect their DIY-manicure skills, try adding gel extensions to your repertoire. Boyce is particularly keen for folks to get their hands on Orly's new Fast Forms product, which makes it possible to create gel extensions quickly and safely at home.</figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/281221/fall-nail-trends-281221-1598040817038-main.800x0uc.png\"><figcaption>\"This kit helps create that perfect curve apex quickly so you don't have to spend a lot of time sculpting it,\" says Boyce. \"When you're creating clear extensions like the glass French tips, you need it to look perfect and precise, and the fast forms make it very easy to do it,\" she explains.</figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/281221/fall-nail-trends-281221-1598035858099-main.1080x1292uc.jpg\"><figcaption>If you consider yourself less savvy in the DIY department, you’re in luck: Press-on styles are back in a big way. “Salons are offering them now, and tons of nail stylists are creating press-ons with nail art,” shares Logan. Nail stickers and wraps are the way to go. “I see that gel nail stickers are one of the most popular emerging products. People like the convenience of an instant manicure,” shares Choi.  Similarly, Hanna is a big fan of nail wraps, which completely cover the nail bed in a single color or with an intricate design. “Nail wraps offer a salon-quality, long-lasting manicure that dries instantly in the comfort of your own home.” </figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/281221/fall-nail-trends-281221-1598043659653-main.800x0uc.jpg\"><figcaption>This is the most on-trend sticker set we've ever seen.</figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/281221/fall-nail-trends-281221-1598043667658-main.800x0uc.jpg\"><figcaption>This brand of nail wraps is the best seller in its category on Amazon. </figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/281221/fall-nail-trends-281221-1598041887592-main.1080x1080uc.jpg\"><figcaption>For fans of nail wraps, Hanna swears by the brand ManiMe. \"They have a really interesting technology that creates custom-cut gel nail wraps, and they collaborate with some really amazing artists,\" she shares. Her favorite is this celestial design with nail artist Hang Nguyen, pictured above.</figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/281221/fall-nail-trends-281221-1598036016180-main.1080x1290uc.jpg\"><figcaption>Nail salons that have been able to open are seeing a rise in popularity of the classic French manicure. Those who have been able to safely see private clients during COVID-19 are also doing more French manicures since the clean, crisp style helps elevate any look. Of course, we know it takes a steady hand to create the perfect tips at home, so this one might be best left to the pros. With that in mind, Boyce reminds us to consider tipping more than usual since many nail techs have been unable to work for several months and salons are limiting their capacity for everyone’s safety.</figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/281221/fall-nail-trends-281221-1598043680896-main.800x0uc.jpg\"><figcaption>Did you know the classic French manicure was invented in 1975 by CEO of Orly International, Jeff Pink? </figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/281221/fall-nail-trends-281221-1598043687146-main.800x0uc.jpg\"><figcaption>This is the white nail polish that started it all. </figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/281221/fall-nail-trends-281221-1598047221240-main.1080x1080uc.jpg\"><figcaption>Finally, for those looking for a polished look without the polish application, Hanna is a big fan of the natural or buffed manicure. “A clean, natural buff is low-maintenance and beautiful,” she says, relating this trend to the more pared-back routines that we’ve seen in the hair and makeup spaces lately.  One critical step in achieving this look is cuticle care. As Hanna reminds us, “healthy cuticles equal healthy nails.” </figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/281221/fall-nail-trends-281221-1598043694606-main.800x0uc.jpg\"><figcaption>At just $2, this seven-way buffer is a must-have for every beauty arsenal.</figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/281221/fall-nail-trends-281221-1598043702086-main.800x0uc.jpg\"><figcaption>Thousands of Amazon reviewers agree that this cuticle oil is heaven-sent. </figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/281221/fall-nail-trends-281221-1598043709133-main.800x0uc.jpg\"><figcaption>It's never a bad idea to upgrade your nailcare kit.</figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/281221/fall-nail-trends-281221-1598036384261-main.1080x1155uc.jpg\"><figcaption>One fall nail trend that all of our pros agreed on was that safety comes first. With that in mind, we asked our experts what to expect as nail salons begin to reopen.  “As a salon owner, my priority is just making sure we protect the client and our team at all costs,” explains Logan.  Choi agrees, sharing, “At JinSoon [spas], we have constructed plexiglass dividers and require all clients and technicians to wear masks and sanitize often, (when arriving, between and during appointments, etc.),” and reminds us that while walk-ins may be welcome, most salon waiting rooms are closed, so it’s best to make an appointment in advance.</figcaption></figure></p><p><em>Up Even if we've been diligent about our <a href=\"https://www.whowhatwear.com/acne-skincare-routine\" target=\"_blank\">nightly skincare routine</a>, wearing our sunscreen, and remembering to remove our makeup post–night out, sometimes it just happens that our skin has seen better, brighter days.</p><p>So we're sharing the best brightening serums that will help transform even the most fatigued of complexions. It's also the top-rated brightening serum sold at Dermstore coming in under $100. I apply it every morning post-cleanser and toner, pre-sunscreen. As the name would suggest, the formula's effectiveness comes thanks to its perfected blend of vitamins C and E (and a strategic dose of ferulic acid to enhance the natural brightening benefits).</figcaption></figure></p><p><figure><img src=\"https://cdn.cliqueinc.com/posts/277276/best-brightening-serums-277276-1549998308626-main.1200x1200uc.jpg\"><figcaption>We try our best not be brand repeaters in these types of roundups, but sometimes a brand is so exceptional or has multiple super-effective formulas suited for different skin types that we just can't resist. I've been using it for months now, and (don't @ me!) I prefer it over the C E Ferulic.
